Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The Cincinnati Bengals and the Kansas City Chiefs are playing a football game. The Bengals have 42 points. The Chiefs have 13 more points. How many points do the two teams have in total?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The Bengals have 42 points
    bengals_points = 42
    #The Chiefs have 13 more points
    chiefs_points = bengals_points + 13
    #The total points is
    total_points = bengals_points + chiefs_points
    return total_points
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam singles titles. 14 of them are in the Australian Open, 3 of them are in the French Open, and 5 of them are in Wimbledon. How many Grand Slam singles titles does she have in the US Open?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam singles titles
    grand_slam_titles = 24
    #14 of them are in the Australian Open
    australian_open_titles = 14
    #3 of them are in the French Open
    french_open_titles = 3
    #5 of them are in Wimbledon
    wimbledon_titles = 5
    #The answer is
    result = grand_slam_titles - australian_open_titles - french_open_titles - wimbledon_titles
    return result
Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 1000 unicorns are in the forest. 200 of them are pink, 300 of them are blue, and the rest are purple. How many unicorns are purple?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1000 unicorns are in the forest
    unicorns_total = 1000
    #200 of them are pink
    unicorns_pink = 200
    #300 of them are blue
    unicorns_blue = 300
    #The rest are purple. The answer is
    unicorns_purple = unicorns_total - unicorns_pink - unicorns_blue
    return unicorns_purple

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A T-Rex is 20 feet tall.  A Brontosaurus is 10 feet tall.  A Velociraptor is 2 feet tall.  How many Velociraptors does it take to equal the height of a T-Rex and a Brontosaurus?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex is 20 feet tall
    t_rex_height = 20
    #A Brontosaurus is 10 feet tall
    brontosaurus_height = 10
    #A Velociraptor is 2 feet tall
    velociraptor_height = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (t_rex_height + brontosaurus_height) / velociraptor_height
    return result
Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: 
The lacrosse team has 120 sticks. 20 of the sticks are for the goalies. 30 of the sticks are for the defenders. 40 of the sticks are for the midfielders. 30 of the sticks are for the attackers. How many sticks are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total sticks
    sticks_total = 120
    #Sticks for goalies
    sticks_goalies = 20
    #Sticks for defenders
    sticks_defenders = 30
    #Sticks for midfielders
    sticks_midfielders = 40
    #Sticks for attackers
    sticks_attackers = 30
    #The answer is
    result = sticks_total - sticks_goalies - sticks_defenders - sticks_midfielders - sticks_attackers
    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total Pokémon in the Kanto region
    total_pokemon = 150
    #Pokémon in the grass
    grass_pokemon = 50
    #Pokémon in the water
    water_pokemon = 30
    #Pokémon in the caves
    cave_pokemon = 20
    #Pokémon in the cities
    city_pokemon = total_pokemon - grass_pokemon - water_pokemon - cave_pokemon
    return city_pokemon

Question: Spiderman can shoot 12 webs per minute.  He can web-sling at 100 miles per hour.  If he is web-slinging for 10 minutes, how far will he travel?
Solution:

    webs_per_minute = 12
    #He can web-sling at 100 miles per hour

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: In the first year, there were 1000 students at Hogwarts.  The next year, 200 more students enrolled.  In the third year, 300 students left.  How many students are there now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #In the first year, there were 1000 students at Hogwarts
    students_first_year = 1000
    #The next year, 200 more students enrolled
    students_enrolled_second_year = 200
    #In the third year, 300 students left
    students_left_third_year = 300
    #The answer is
    result = students_first_year + students_enrolled_second_year - students_left_third_year
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response: 

Question: 12 of the 21 dogs in the park are beagles. 2 of the 12 cats in the park are Siamese. 1 of the 19 birds in the park is a pigeon. What is the total number of beagles, Siamese cats, and pigeons in the park?

Solution:

def solution():
    #4 of the 21 dogs in the park are beagles
    beagles = 4
    #2 of the 12 cats in the park are Siamese
    siamese_cats = 2
    #1 of the 19 birds in the park is a pigeon
    pigeons = 1
    #The answer is
    result = beagles + siamese_cats + pigeons
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 20 players. 6 of them are forwards, 8 of them are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many defenders are on the field hockey team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 20
    #Forwards
    forwards = 6
    #Midfielders
    midfielders = 8
    #Defenders
    defenders = total_players - forwards - midfielders
    return defenders
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 

Question: 

The cheer leading squad has 20 members. 10 of them are in the 10th grade, 6 of them are in the 11th grade, and the rest are in the 12th grade. How many of them are in the 12th grade?

Solution:

def solution():
    #The cheer leading squad has 20 members
    squad_members = 20
    #10 of them are in the 10th grade
    tenth_grade_members = 10
    #6 of them are in the 11th grade
    eleventh_grade_members = 6
    #The rest are in the 12th grade
    twelfth_grade_members = squad_members - tenth_grade_members - eleventh_grade_members
    #The answer is
    result = twelfth_grade_members
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: 3000 M&Ms are in a candy dish. 1200 of them are red, 600 of them are blue, 400 of them are green, and the rest are yellow. How many M&Ms are yellow?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of M&Ms
    total_mms = 3000
    #The number of red, blue, and green M&Ms
    red_mms = 1200
    blue_mms = 600
    green_mms = 400
    #The rest of the M&Ms are yellow
    yellow_mms = total_mms - red_mms - blue_mms - green_mms
    return yellow_mms

Question: A field hockey team has 12 players. 3 of the players are on the forward line, 4 are on the midfield line, and 5 are on the defensive line. How many players are not on the forward, midfield, or defensive lines?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Forward line players
    forward_line_players = 3
    #Midfield line players
    midfield_line_players = 4
    #Defensive line players
    defensive_line_players = 5
    #Players not on the forward, midfield, or defensive lines
    other_line_players = total_players - forward_line_players - midfield_line_players - defensive_line_players
    return other_line_players

Topic: cars ### Response: 

Question: A 4-lane highway has 3,000 cars per lane. A 2-lane highway has 2,000 cars per lane. How many more cars are on the 4-lane highway than the 2-lane highway?

Solution:
def solution():
    #4-lane highway has 3,000 cars per lane
    four_lane_cars_per_lane = 3000
    #2-lane highway has 2,000 cars per lane
    two_lane_cars_per_lane = 2000
    #4-lane highway has 4 lanes
    four_lane_lanes = 4
    #2-lane highway has 2 lanes
    two_lane_lanes = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (four_lane_cars_per_lane * four_lane_lanes) - (two_lane_cars_per_lane * two_lane_lanes)
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: 20 cats are at the cat cafe. 10 of the cats are black. 6 of the cats are white. 4 of the cats are both black and white. How many cats are neither black nor white?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 cats are at the cat cafe
    cats = 20
    #10 of the cats are black
    black_cats = 10
    #6 of the cats are white
    white_cats = 6
    #4 of the cats are both black and white
    both_cats = 4
    #The answer is
    result = cats - black_cats - white_cats + both_cats
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A 400-car freight train is 4 miles long. A 200-car passenger train is 2 miles long. How many miles long is a 300-car train?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 400-car freight train is 4 miles long
    freight_train_cars = 400
    freight_train_length = 4
    #A 200-car passenger train is 2 miles long
    passenger_train_cars = 200
    passenger_train_length = 2
    #A 300-car train is
    train_cars = 300
    #The answer is
    result = (freight_train_cars * freight_train_length + passenger_train_cars * passenger_train_length) / train_cars
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 12 players. 3 of them are attackers, 3 are midfielders, 3 are defenders, and 3 are goalies. The attackers and midfielders each have 2 sticks. The defenders and goalies each have 1 stick. How many sticks does the team have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 12 players
    players = 12
    #The attackers and midfielders each have 2 sticks
    attackers_sticks = 3 * 2
    midfielders_sticks = 3 * 2
    #The defenders and goalies each have 1 stick
    defenders_sticks = 3 * 1
    goalies_sticks = 3 * 1
    #The answer is
    result = attackers_sticks + midfielders_sticks + defenders_sticks + goalies_sticks
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: A Minecraft world has 12000 blocks. 30% of the blocks are stone. 20% of the stone is smooth stone. 10% of the smooth stone is mossy smooth stone. How many mossy smooth stones are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of blocks
    total_blocks = 12000
    #Percentage of stone blocks
    stone_percentage = 30/100
    #Percentage of smooth stone
    smooth_stone_percentage = 20/100
    #Percentage of mossy smooth stone
    mossy_smooth_stone_percentage = 10/100
    #Calculate the number of mossy smooth stones
    mossy_smooth_stones = total_blocks * stone_percentage * smooth_stone_percentage * mossy_smooth_stone_percentage
    return mossy_smooth_stones

    #He uses 10 vibranium ingots to make a new suit
    vibranium_ingots_suit = 10
    #He then uses 20 vibranium ingots to make a new car
    vibranium_ingots_car = 20
    #The answer is
    result = vibranium_ingots_total - vibranium_ingots_suit - vibranium_ingots_car
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 
A volleyball team is 6 players. 
3 of the players are 16 years old. 
2 of the players are 17 years old. 
1 of the players is 18 years old. 
What is the average age of the team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #3 of the players are 16 years old
    players_16 = 3
    #2 of the players are 17 years old
    players_17 = 2
    #1 of the players is 18 years old
    players_18 = 1
    #The average age is
    average_age = (players_16 * 16 + players_17 * 17 + players_18 * 18) / 6
    return average_age

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza is cut into 8 slices. 2 of the slices have mushrooms, 3 of the slices have pepperoni, and 1 of the slices has both mushrooms and pepperoni. How many slices of pizza do not have mushrooms or pepperoni?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total slices
    total_slices = 8
    #Slices with mushrooms
    mushroom_slices = 2
    #Slices with pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = 3
    #Slices with both mushrooms and pepperoni
    both_slices = 1
    #Slices without mushrooms or pepperoni
    result = total_slices - mushroom_slices - pepperoni_slices + both_slices
    return result
Topic: ice cream ### Response: 

Question: 300 people are in line for ice cream. 150 of them order a scoop of ice cream, 125 of them order 2 scoops, and the rest order 3 scoops. How many scoops of ice cream are ordered in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #300 people are in line for ice cream
    people_in_line = 300
    #150 of them order a scoop of ice cream
    scoop_of_ice_cream = 150
    #125 of them order 2 scoops
    two_scoops = 125
    #The rest order 3 scoops
    three_scoops = people_in_line - scoop_of_ice_cream - two_scoops
    #The answer is
    result = scoop_of_ice_cream + two_scoops + three_scoops
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: 

The 49ers and the Rams are playing a football game. 

In the first half, the 49ers scored 14 points. 

In the second half, the 49ers scored 10 more points than the Rams, who scored 24. 

How many points did the 49ers score in the game?
Solution:
def solution():

    # 49ers' score in the first half
    first_half_score = 14

    # Rams' score in the second half
    rams_second_half_score = 24

    # 49ers' score in the second half is 10 more than the Rams'
    second_half_score = rams_second_half_score + 10

    # 49ers' total score is the sum of their first and second half scores
    total_score = first_half_score + second_half_score

    return total_score

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman is 8 feet tall.  He is 20% taller than Batman.  How tall is Batman? (There are 12 inches in a foot.)
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman is 8 feet tall
    superman_height = 8
    #He is 20% taller than Batman
    batman_height_percent = 100 - 20
    #The answer is
    result = (superman_height * 12) * (batman_height_percent / 100)
    return result
Topic: football ### Response: 
Question:
Tom Brady has 1500 passing yards. He gains 300 yards per game for the next 5 games. How many passing yards does he have now?

Solution:

    passing_yards_initial = 1500
    #He gains 300 yards per game for the next 5 games
    yards_per_game = 300
    #There are 5 games
    num_games = 5
    #He gained
    yards_gained = yards_per_game * num_games
    #The answer is
    result = passing_yards_initial + yards_gained
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: 128 pizzas were sliced into 4 slices each. 16 of the slices were given to the pizza chef. 24 slices were given to the pizza delivery drivers. How many slices of pizza are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #128 pizzas were sliced
    pizzas = 128
    #Each pizza was sliced into 4 slices
    slices_per_pizza = 4
    #16 slices were given to the pizza chef
    slices_given_to_chef = 16
    #24 slices were given to the pizza delivery drivers
    slices_given_to_drivers = 24
    #The answer is
    result = pizzas * slices_per_pizza - slices_given_to_chef - slices_given_to_drivers
    return result

    players = 11
    #3 of the players are forwards
    forwards = 3
    #5 of the players are midfielders
    midfielders = 5
    #3 of the players are defenders
    defenders = 3
    #The number of players who are not forwards is
    not_forwards = players - forwards
    return not_forwards

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: 1200 people are on a 747. 1/3 of the people are in first class. 1/6 of the people are in business class. 1/4 of the people are in premium economy. The rest are in economy. How many people are in economy?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1200 people are on a 747
    total_people = 1200
    #1/3 of the people are in first class
    first_class_people = total_people / 3
    #1/6 of the people are in business class
    business_class_people = total_people / 6
    #1/4 of the people are in premium economy
    premium_economy_people = total_people / 4
    #The rest are in economy
    economy_people = total_people - first_class_people - business_class_people - premium_economy_people
    return economy_people

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey game lasts for 70 minutes. 
The first half is 35 minutes, and the second half is 35 minutes. 
There is a 10-minute break at halftime. 
How long is the game in hours?

Solution:
def solution():
    # A field hockey game lasts for 70 minutes.
    # The first half is 35 minutes, and the second half is 35 minutes.
    # There is a 10-minute break at halftime.
    # 70 minutes is 1.16 hours.

    def time_to_hours(minutes):
        return minutes / 60

    game_length = 70
    first_half = 35
    second_half = 35
    halftime = 10
    total_hours = (first_half + second_half + halftime) / 60
    return total_hours

Topic: soccer ### Response: 

Question:
The US soccer team has 22 players. 11 of the players are on the field at a time. 3 of the players are goalies. 2 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are midfielders. The rest of the players are defenders. How many defenders are there?

Solution:

def solution():
    #The US soccer team has 22 players
    total_players = 22
    #11 of the players are on the field at a time
    players_on_field = 11
    #3 of the players are goalies
    goalies = 3
    #2 of the players are forwards
    forwards = 2
    #6 of the players are midfielders
    midfielders = 6
    #The rest of the players are defenders. The answer is
    defenders = total_players - players_on_field + goalies + forwards + midfielders
    return defenders

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: A 747 can fly 10,000 miles in 20 hours.  A 777 can fly 12,000 miles in 25 hours.  How many more miles per hour can a 747 fly than a 777?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 747 can fly 10,000 miles in 20 hours
    miles_747 = 10000
    hours_747 = 20
    #A 777 can fly 12,000 miles in 25 hours
    miles_777 = 12000
    hours_777 = 25
    #The answer is
    result = (miles_747 / hours_747) - (miles_777 / hours_777)
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza is cut into 8 slices. 2 of the slices have pepperoni, 3 of the slices have mushrooms, and 1 of the slices has both pepperoni and mushrooms. How many slices of pizza have neither pepperoni nor mushrooms?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza is cut into 8 slices
    slices_total = 8
    #2 of the slices have pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 2
    #3 of the slices have mushrooms
    slices_mushrooms = 3
    #1 of the slices has both pepperoni and mushrooms
    slices_both = 1
    #The answer is
    result = slices_total - slices_pepperoni - slices_mushrooms + slices_both
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel is a superhero. She can punch 30 times per second. How many punches can she throw in 5 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel can punch 30 times per second
    punches_per_second = 30
    #There are 60 seconds in a minute
    seconds_per_minute = 60
    #5 minutes is 300 seconds
    minutes = 5
    seconds_in_5_minutes = minutes * seconds_per_minute
    #She can punch
    punches_in_5_minutes = punches_per_second * seconds_in_5_minutes
    #punches in 5 minutes. The answer is
    result = punches_in_5_minutes
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: A swimmer swims 12 laps every day. It takes 20 minutes to swim one lap. How many hours does the swimmer spend swimming in 5 days?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A swimmer swims 12 laps every day
    laps_per_day = 12
    #It takes 20 minutes to swim one lap
    minutes_per_lap = 20
    #5 days
    days = 5
    #The answer is
    result = (laps_per_day * minutes_per_lap * days) / 60
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: 
The field hockey team has 16 players. 8 of them are forwards, 6 of them are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. 2 of the defenders are goalies.  How many non-goalie defenders are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 16
    #Forwards
    forwards = 8
    #Midfielders
    midfielders = 6
    #Defenders
    defenders = total_players - forwards - midfielders
    #Defender goalies
    defender_goalies = 2
    #Non-goalie defenders
    non_goalie_defenders = defenders - defender_goalies
    return non_goalie_defenders

    #4 years ago, he was 2/3 as old as Sasuke

    sasuke_age_4_years_ago = naruto_age_4_years_ago / (2/3)
    #Sasuke is now
    sasuke_age = sasuke_age_4_years_ago + 4
    return sasuke_age

3 of the players are defenders. 
How many players are neither forwards nor defenders?
Solution:
def solution():
    # total players
    total_players = 11
    # forwards
    forwards = 8
    # defenders
    defenders = 3
    # neither forwards nor defenders
    neither_forwards_nor_defenders = total_players - forwards - defenders
    return neither_forwards_nor_defenders
Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza is cut into 8 slices. 2 of the slices have pepperoni, 3 of the slices have mushrooms, and 1 of the slices has both pepperoni and mushrooms. How many slices of pizza have toppings?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza is cut into 8 slices
    slices = 8
    #2 of the slices have pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = 2
    #3 of the slices have mushrooms
    mushroom_slices = 3
    #1 of the slices has both pepperoni and mushrooms
    both_slices = 1
    #The answer is
    result = pepperoni_slices + mushroom_slices - both_slices
    return result
Topic: soccer ### Response:

    soccer_players = 11
    #Number of goalies
    goalies = 3
    #Number of defenders

    #Number of forwards is

    return forwards
Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: 
A 25-meter pool is 1.25 fathoms deep. 
Each fathom is 6 feet. 
How many feet is the pool deep?
Solution:
def solution():
    # 1 fathom is 6 feet
    fathom_to_feet = 6
    # 1 pool is 1.25 fathoms deep
    fathoms_deep = 1.25
    # The pool is
    feet_deep = fathoms_deep * fathom_to_feet
    return feet_deep

How many attendees are from the United States?

    eu_percentage = 0.15
    au_percentage = 0.10
    rotw_percentage = 0.20

Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 12 unicorns ate 120 apples. 10 unicorns ate 100 carrots. 8 unicorns ate 80 pears. How many fruits in total did the unicorns eat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #12 unicorns ate 120 apples
    unicorns_apples = 12 * 120
    #10 unicorns ate 100 carrots
    unicorns_carrots = 10 * 100
    #8 unicorns ate 80 pears
    unicorns_pears = 8 * 80
    #The answer is
    result = unicorns_apples + unicorns_carrots + unicorns_pears
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: I ate 3 of the 50 cookies in the jar. I then ate 20% of the remaining cookies. How many cookies do I have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Initial number of cookies
    cookies_initial = 50
    #Cookies eaten
    cookies_eaten_1 = 3
    #Remaining cookies
    cookies_remaining_1 = cookies_initial - cookies_eaten_1
    #Cookies eaten as 20% of the remaining cookies
    cookies_eaten_2 = cookies_remaining_1 * 0.20
    #Remaining cookies
    cookies_remaining_2 = cookies_remaining_1 - cookies_eaten_2
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_remaining_2
    return result

    spiderman_web_sling_feet = 1200
    #He can web-sling 300 feet per minute
    spiderman_web_sling_speed = 300
    #The answer is
    time = spiderman_web_sling_feet / spiderman_web_sling_speed
    return time

    cats_2 = 3

    kittens_3 = 3

    return result

    dogs_initial = 200
    #100 more dogs show up
    dogs_showed_up = 100
    #25% of the dogs at the dog park are barking
    barking_dogs_percentage = 0.25
    #The answer is

    return result

How many more points does he have than rebounds and assists combined?

Topic: Barbie ### Response: 
Question: Barbie has 1000. She spends 200 on a new car, 100 on a new wardrobe, and 25% of her remaining money on a new apartment. How much money does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barbie started with 1000
    money_initial = 1000
    #She spent 200 on a new car
    car_cost = 200
    #She spent 100 on a new wardrobe
    wardrobe_cost = 100
    #She spent 25% of her remaining money on a new apartment
    apartment_cost = (money_initial - car_cost - wardrobe_cost) * 0.25
    #The answer is
    result = money_initial - car_cost - wardrobe_cost - apartment_cost
    return result

    #He uses 20 of them in each of his 5 fights
    fights = 5
    #The answer is
    result = vibranium_daggers - (20 * fights)
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The Lakers have 12 players. 4 of them are 2-meter-tall centers, 5 of them are 1.9-meter-tall forwards, and 3 of them are 1.8-meter-tall guards. How tall is the average Laker?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of players of each height
    players_2m = 4
    players_1.9m = 5
    players_1.8m = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (players_2m * 2 + players_1.9m * 1.9 + players_1.8m * 1.8) / total_players
    return result

Question: 

Steve, the main character in Minecraft, is in the Nether. He has 100 health points. 20% of his health points are lost in the first 5 minutes. 30% of his health points are lost in the second 5 minutes. How many health points does he have left?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Steve has 100 health points
    health_points = 100
    #20% of his health points are lost in the first 5 minutes
    health_points_lost_first_5_minutes = health_points * 0.20
    #30% of his health points are lost in the second 5 minutes
    health_points_lost_second_5_minutes = health_points * 0.30
    #The answer is
    result = health_points - health_points_lost_first_5_minutes - health_points_lost_second_5_minutes
    return result

Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America is a superhero. He can punch 1000 times a second. He can also punch 1000 times a second with his other fist. How many punches can he throw in 5 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America can punch 1000 times a second
    punches_per_second = 1000
    #He can punch with both fists
    fists = 2
    #There are 60 seconds in a minute
    seconds_per_minute = 60
    #There are 5 minutes in 5 minutes
    minutes = 5
    #The answer is
    result = punches_per_second * fists * seconds_per_minute * minutes
    return result

Topic: Black Panther ### Response: 

Question:
Black Panther can punch 1200 times in 1 hour. 

How many punches can he throw in 30 days?

Solution:

def solution():

  # Black Panther can punch 1200 times in 1 hour
  punches_per_hour = 1200

  # 1 day is 24 hours, so 30 days is 30*24 hours
  days = 30

  # calculate the number of punches he can throw in 30 days
  punches_30_days = punches_per_hour * days

  # return the answer
  return punches_30_days

    total_cars = 500
    #Cars of each color
    red_cars = 200
    blue_cars = 100
    black_cars = 100
    silver_cars = 50
    green_cars = 50
    #Cars that are not red, blue, black, silver, or green

Topic: cookies ### Response: 

Question: 120 cookies are to be baked and packaged in 12-cookie bags. 20% of the bags will be given away as free samples. How many bags of cookies will be sold?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cookies
    total_cookies = 120
    #Cookies per bag
    cookies_per_bag = 12
    #Bags to be given away
    bags_given_away = 0.2
    #Bags to be sold
    bags_sold = (1 - bags_given_away)
    #The answer is
    result = total_cookies / cookies_per_bag * bags_sold
    return result

    followers = 10000

Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 
Question: In the Super Mario game, the mushroom is worth 1000 points, the star is worth 2000 points, and the flower is worth 3000 points. 
If Mario gets 5 mushrooms, 4 stars, and 2 flowers, how many points does he have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Mushroom is worth 1000 points
    mushroom_points = 1000
    #Star is worth 2000 points
    star_points = 2000
    #Flower is worth 3000 points
    flower_points = 3000
    #Mario gets 5 mushrooms, 4 stars, and 2 flowers
    mushrooms = 5
    stars = 4
    flowers = 2
    #The answer is
    result = mushrooms * mushroom_points + stars * star_points + flowers * flower_points
    return result
Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: 
The T-Rex is the largest dinosaur. It is 2000 pounds. The Brontosaurus is 2/5 the size of the T-Rex. The Velociraptor is 1/100 the size of the Brontosaurus. How much does the Velociraptor weigh?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The T-Rex weighs 2000 pounds
    t_rex_weight = 2000
    #The Brontosaurus is 2/5 the size of the T-Rex
    brontosaurus_weight = (2/5) * t_rex_weight
    #The Velociraptor is 1/100 the size of the Brontosaurus
    velociraptor_weight = (1/100) * brontosaurus_weight
    #The answer is
    result = velociraptor_weight
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza is cut into 12 slices. 3/4 of the slices are pepperoni. 1/4 of the slices are mushroom. 1/2 of the mushroom slices also have extra cheese. How many slices of pizza have pepperoni, mushroom, and extra cheese?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza is cut into 12 slices
    pizza_slices = 12
    #3/4 of the slices are pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = pizza_slices * 3/4
    #1/4 of the slices are mushroom
    mushroom_slices = pizza_slices * 1/4
    #1/2 of the mushroom slices also have extra cheese
    extra_cheese_slices = mushroom_slices / 2
    #The answer is
    result = pepperoni_slices + mushroom_slices + extra_cheese_slices
    return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry, Ron, and Hermione all have 100 house points. 

If Harry, Ron, and Hermione all lose 25, 30, and 20 house points, respectively, how many house points do they have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry, Ron, and Hermione all have 100 house points
    house_points_initial = 100
    #Harry, Ron, and Hermione all lose 25, 30, and 20 house points, respectively
    house_points_lost_harry = 25
    house_points_lost_ron = 30
    house_points_lost_hermione = 20
    #The answer is
    result = (house_points_initial - house_points_lost_harry - house_points_lost_ron - house_points_lost_hermione)
    return result

    #2 of the slices have pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 2
    #5 of the slices have mushrooms
    slices_mushrooms = 5
    #3 of the slices have both pepperoni and mushrooms
    slices_both = 3
    #The answer is
    result = slices - slices_pepperoni - slices_mushrooms + slices_both
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: There are 20 Power Rangers. 2 of them are Red Rangers, 4 of them are Blue Rangers, 7 of them are Pink Rangers, and the rest are Yellow Rangers. How many Yellow Rangers are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of Power Rangers
    total_rangers = 20
    #Number of Red, Blue, and Pink Rangers
    red_rangers = 2
    blue_rangers = 4
    pink_rangers = 7
    #Number of Yellow Rangers is the total minus the Red, Blue, and Pink Rangers
    yellow_rangers = total_rangers - red_rangers - blue_rangers - pink_rangers
    return yellow_rangers

Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James is 6 feet, 8 inches tall
    lebron_height = 6.8
    #20% of the other players on his team are taller than him
    taller_percent = 20
    #There are 10 players on his team
    total_players = 10
    #20% of 10 is
    taller_players = (taller_percent / 100) * total_players
    #The answer is
    result = taller_players
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 

Question: A 10-car train is in a train yard. 

Each day, 2 more cars are added. 

How many cars are in the train yard at the end of 5 days?

Solution:
def solution():
    #There were initially 10 cars
    cars_initial = 10
    #They added 2 more each day
    cars_per_day = 2
    #There are 5 days
    num_days = 5
    #There were
    cars_added = cars_per_day * num_days
    #cars added. The answer is
    result = cars_initial + cars_added
    return result

    vanilla_cakes = cakes - chocolate_cakes - strawberry_cakes
    return vanilla_cakes

def solution():

    money_initial = 1000
    #He withdrew 200.00 for a new outfit
    outfit_cost = 200
    #He withdrew 300.00 for a new car
    car_cost = 300
    #He withdrew 100.00 for a new house
    house_cost = 100

Solution:
def solution():
    #The total distance is 200 miles
    total_distance = 200
    #The train goes 60 mph for 1.5 hours
    mph1 = 60
    hours1 = 1.5
    #The train goes 80 mph for 1.5 hours
    mph2 = 80
    hours2 = 1.5
    #The train goes 40 mph for the rest of the trip
    mph3 = 40
    #The answer is
    result = (mph1 * hours1) + (mph2 * hours2) + (total_distance - (mph1 * hours1)

There are 20 dogs in a dog park. 10 of the dogs are dachshunds, 5 are corgis, and the rest are beagles. How many beagles are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of dogs
    total_dogs = 20
    #Number of dachshunds
    dachshunds = 10
    #Number of corgis
    corgis = 5
    #The answer is
    beagles = total_dogs - dachshunds - corgis
    return beagles
Topic: Naruto ### Response: 
Question: Naruto ate 169 ramen noodles. Sasuke ate 11 more than Naruto. How many ramen noodles did they eat in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Naruto ate 169 ramen noodles
    naruto_ramen = 169
    #Sasuke ate 11 more than Naruto
    sasuke_ramen = naruto_ramen + 11
    #The answer is
    result = naruto_ramen + sasuke_ramen
    return result
Topic: pizza ### Response: 
def solution():
    #A pizza is cut into 12 slices. 
    #If 3 of the slices are pepperoni, 
    #4 of the slices are mushroom, 
    #2 of the slices are onion, 
    #and 2 of the slices are green pepper, 
    #how many slices are there of each topping?
    pizza_slices = 12
    pepperoni_slices = 3
    mushroom_slices = 4
    onion_slices = 2
    green_pepper_slices = 2
    #The answer is
    result = pizza_slices - pepperoni_slices - mushroom_slices - onion_slices - green_pepper_slices
    return result
Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 12 repulsor rays. He uses 3 of them to blast the Hulk. He then uses 2 of them to blast the Abomination. How many repulsor rays does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 12 repulsor rays
    repulsor_rays_initial = 12
    #He uses 3 of them to blast the Hulk
    repulsor_rays_used_hulk = 3
    #He then uses 2 of them to blast the Abomination
    repulsor_rays_used_abomination = 2
    #The answer is
    result = repulsor_rays_initial - repulsor_rays_used_hulk - repulsor_rays_used_abomination
    return result
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 22 Grand Slam titles. 13 of them are in singles, 7 of them are in women's doubles, and the rest are in mixed doubles. How many Grand Slam titles does Serena Williams have in mixed doubles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 22 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles = 22
    #13 of them are in singles
    singles_titles = 13
    #7 of them are in women's doubles
    womens_doubles_titles = 7
    #The rest are in mixed doubles. The answer is
    mixed_doubles_titles = grand_slam_titles - singles_titles - womens_doubles_titles
    return mixed_doubles_titles
Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: A Creeper has 200 health points. A Skeleton has 100 health points. A Zombie has 150 health points. How many health points do 2 Creepers, 3 Skeletons, and 2 Zombies have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A Creeper has 200 health points
    creeper_health = 200
    #A Skeleton has 100 health points
    skeleton_health = 100
    #A Zombie has 150 health points
    zombie_health = 150
    #The answer is
    result = 2*creeper_health + 3*skeleton_health + 2*zombie_health
    return result

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 
Question: Taylor Swift has 2000 3-point shots. She has 1000 more 2-point shots than 3-point shots. She has 2000 free throws. How many shots does she have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift has 2000 3-point shots
    three_point_shots = 2000
    #She has 1000 more 2-point shots than 3-point shots
    two_point_shots = three_point_shots + 1000
    #She has 2000 free throws
    free_throws = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = three_point_shots + two_point_shots + free_throws
    return result
Topic: Superman ### Response: 

Question: 
Superman can punch 1000 times in 10 seconds. 
How many punches can he throw in 50 seconds?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can punch 1000 times in 10 seconds
    punches_per_second = 1000 / 10
    #He can punch
    punches_in_50_seconds = punches_per_second * 50
    #The answer is
    result = punches_in_50_seconds
    return result
Topic: Batman ### Response: 

Question: Batman has 30 batarangs.  He buys 20 more batarangs.  He then gives 12 batarangs to Robin.  How many batarangs does he have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman started with 30 batarangs
    batarangs_initial = 30
    #He bought 20 more
    batarangs_bought = 20
    #He gave 12 to Robin
    batarangs_given = 12
    #The answer is
    result = batarangs_initial + batarangs_bought - batarangs_given
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 
A volleyball team has 12 players. 
4 of the players are setters, 
3 of the players are liberos, 
3 of the players are outside hitters, and 
2 of the players are middle blockers. 
How many players on the team are not setters, liberos, outside hitters, or middle blockers?
Solution:
def solution():
    #12 players
    players = 12
    #4 of the players are setters
    setters = 4
    #3 of the players are liberos
    liberos = 3
    #3 of the players are outside hitters
    outside_hitters = 3
    #2 of the players are middle blockers
    middle_blockers = 2
    #The answer is
    result = players - setters - liberos - outside_hitters - middle_blockers
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: 
The cheerleading squad has 20 members. 
They are in 5 formations. 
The first formation has 4 members. 
The second formation has 3 members. 
The third formation has 5 members. 
The fourth formation has 2 members. 
The fifth formation has 6 members. 
How many members are in the largest formation?
Solution:
def solution():
    # The number of members in the first formation
    first_formation = 4
    # The number of members in the second formation
    second_formation = 3
    # The number of members in the third formation
    third_formation = 5
    # The number of members in the fourth formation
    fourth_formation = 2
    # The number of members in the fifth formation
    fifth_formation = 6
    # The answer is
    result = max(first_formation, second_formation, third_formation, fourth_formation, fifth_formation)
    return result

Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James is 6'9" tall. 
He's 36 years old. 
He's 20 years older than his son. 
How tall is his son in feet?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James is 6'9" tall
    lebron_height_in_feet = 6.9
    #He's 36 years old
    lebron_age = 36
    #He's 20 years older than his son
    son_age = lebron_age - 20
    #His son is
    son_height_in_feet = lebron_height_in_feet * (1 - (1 / 20) * son_age)
    #The answer is
    result = son_height_in_feet
    return result
Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: A 747 can hold 366 passengers. A 777 can hold 300 passengers. How many more passengers can 747s hold than 777s if there are 25 747s and 12 777s?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 747 can hold 366 passengers
    passengers_747 = 366
    #A 777 can hold 300 passengers
    passengers_777 = 300
    #There are 25 747s
    planes_747 = 25
    #12 777s
    planes_777 = 12
    #The answer is
    result = (passengers_747 * planes_747) - (passengers_777 * planes_777)
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can fly at a speed of 1,000 miles per hour. He flies from Metropolis to Gotham City, which is 200 miles away. How long does it take him to get there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly at a speed of 1,000 miles per hour
    superman_speed = 1000
    #He flies from Metropolis to Gotham City, which is 200 miles away
    distance = 200
    #The answer is
    result = distance / superman_speed
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 
A volleyball team has 12 players. 
4 of the players are 18 years old. 
3 of the players are 19 years old. 
2 of the players are 20 years old. 
1 of the players is 21 years old. 
2 of the players are 22 years old. 
How many of the players are not 18, 19, 20, or 21 years old?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of players who are 18, 19, 20, and 21
    players_18 = 4
    players_19 = 3
    players_20 = 2
    players_21 = 1
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - players_18 - players_19 - players_20 - players_21
    return result

Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 
Question: In the Mushroom Kingdom, there are 300 Toads. 100 of them are in the Mushroom Village, 50 of them are in the Flower Fields, and 20 of them are in the Lava Pits.  How many Toads are not in any of these three places?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of Toads
    total_toads = 300
    #The number of Toads in the Mushroom Village
    toads_mushroom_village = 100
    #The number of Toads in the Flower Fields
    toads_flower_fields = 50
    #The number of Toads in the Lava Pits
    toads_lava_pits = 20
    #The answer is
    result = total_toads - toads_mushroom_village - toads_flower_fields - toads_lava_pits
    return result

Question: Thor is 1000 years old. 100 of those years were spent in Asgard. 400 of those years were spent on Earth. 100 of those years were spent in other realms. How many years has Thor spent in space?

    years_old = 1000
    #100 of those years were spent in Asgard
    asgard_years = 100
    #400 of those years were spent on Earth

Topic: Batman ### Response:

    batarangs_initial = 200
    #He used 20 per night
    batarangs_used_per_night = 20
    #There are 5 nights
    num_nights = 5
    #The answer is
    result = batarangs_initial - batarangs_used_per_night * num_nights
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: 
The 3:15 PM train from Penn Station to Union Station is 200 miles long. It travels at 60 miles per hour for 1.5 hours, then at 40 miles per hour for the rest of the trip. How long does the train take to get to Union Station?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The train is 200 miles long
    train_distance = 200
    #It travels at 60 miles per hour for 1.5 hours
    speed1 = 60
    time1 = 1.5
    #Then at 40 miles per hour for the rest of the trip
    speed2 = 40
    #The answer is
    result = (train_distance * time1 / speed1) + (train_distance * (1 - time1) / speed2)
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 
A volleyball team has 12 players. 
3 of the players are in the 12th grade, 
5 of the players are in the 11th grade, 
2 of the players are in the 10th grade, 
and the rest of the players are in the 9th grade. 
How many players are in the 9th grade?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of 12th graders
    twelfth_graders = 3
    #Number of 11th graders
    eleventh_graders = 5
    #Number of 10th graders
    tenth_graders = 2
    #The rest are in the 9th grade. The answer is
    ninth_graders = total_players - twelfth_graders - eleventh_graders - tenth_graders
    return ninth_graders

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 

Question: A field hockey team has 12 players. 4 of them are forwards, 6 of them are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many defenders are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of forwards and midfielders
    forwards = 4
    midfielders = 6
    #Number of defenders is
    defenders = total_players - forwards - midfielders
    return defenders

    #He used 100 spider webs to capture 5 criminals
    spider_webs_used_1 = 100
    #He used 10 spider webs to capture 2 more criminals

    #The answer is

Question: Steve has 1000 Minecraft coins. He spends 200 coins on a new outfit, 300 coins on a new pickaxe, and 100 coins on a new shovel. How many coins does he have left?

    #and the rest are blockers. 
    #How many blockers are there?

    total_players = 12
    setters = 3
    hitters = 5
    liberos = 2

    blockers = total_players - setters - hitters - liberos

    return blockers

2000 cats were at the 1996 Cat Show in Atlanta. 1000 more cats came on the second day. 2000 more cats came on the third day. 1000 cats left on the fourth day. How many cats were there on the fourth day?

Solution:

    cats_initial = 2000
    #1000 more cats came on the second day
    cats_second_day = 1000
    #2000 more cats came on the third day
    cats_third_day = 2000
    #1000 cats left on the fourth day
    cats_left_fourth_day = 1000
    #The answer is

    return
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A train is 2000 feet long. 20% of the train is the engine, and 30% of the train is the caboose. How long is the rest of the train?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A train is 2000 feet long
    train_length = 2000
    #20% of the train is the engine, and 30% of the train is the caboose
    engine_length = train_length * 0.20
    caboose_length = train_length * 0.30
    #The rest of the train is
    result = train_length - engine_length - caboose_length
    return result

Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 

Question: Super Mario has 1000 coins. He spends 200 coins on a mushroom. He then spends 3/5 of the remaining coins on a fire flower. How many coins does he have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Super Mario started with 1000 coins
    coins_initial = 1000
    #He spent 200 coins on a mushroom
    coins_mushroom = 200
    #He then spent 3/5 of the remaining coins on a fire flower
    coins_fire_flower = 3/5 * (coins_initial - coins_mushroom)
    #The answer is
    result = coins_initial - coins_mushroom - coins_fire_flower
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The New England Patriots are 12-2. The Denver Broncos are 10-4. The Baltimore Ravens are 11-3. The Patriots, Broncos, and Ravens all win their next game. How many wins does the team with the most wins have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The New England Patriots are 12-2
    patriots_wins = 12
    #The Denver Broncos are 10-4
    broncos_wins = 10
    #The Baltimore Ravens are 11-3
    ravens_wins = 11
    #All three teams win their next game
    next_game_wins = 3
    #The answer is
    result = max(patriots_wins + next_game_wins, broncos_wins + next_game_wins, ravens_wins + next_game_wins)
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A T-Rex has 60 teeth. A Brachiosaurus has 20 more teeth than a T-Rex. A Velociraptor has 40 fewer teeth than a Brachiosaurus. How many teeth do the three dinosaurs have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex has 60 teeth
    t_rex_teeth = 60
    #A Brachiosaurus has 20 more teeth than a T-Rex
    brachiosaurus_teeth = t_rex_teeth + 20
    #A Velociraptor has 40 fewer teeth than a Brachiosaurus
    velociraptor_teeth = brachiosaurus_teeth - 40
    #The answer is
    result = t_rex_teeth + brachiosaurus_teeth + velociraptor_teeth
    return result

A Skeleton has 100 health points. 
A Zombie has 150 health points. 
How many Creepers, Skeletons, and Zombies with full health can you kill with 1200 health points?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A Creeper has 200 health points
    creeper_health = 200
    #A Skeleton has 100 health points
    skeleton_health = 100
    #A Zombie has 150 health points
    zombie_health = 150
    #You have 1200 health points
    health_points = 1200
    #The answer is
    result = health_points // (creeper_health + skeleton_health + zombie_health)
    return result

    passengers_5_777s = 5 * passengers_777

Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James, the NBA star, is 6.9 feet tall.  He wears shoes that are 1.5 inches thick.  How tall is he in inches?  (1 foot is 12 inches)
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron's height in feet
    lebron_height_feet = 6.9
    #LeBron's shoe thickness in inches
    shoe_thickness = 1.5
    #1 foot is 12 inches
    feet_to_inches = 12
    #LeBron's height in inches is
    lebron_height_inches = lebron_height_feet * feet_to_inches + shoe_thickness
    return lebron_height_inches

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 5000 armor pieces. He uses 2000 of them to build a new suit of armor. He then uses 1/4 of the remaining armor pieces to build a second suit of armor. How many armor pieces does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 5000 armor pieces
    armor_pieces_total = 5000
    #He uses 2000 of them to build a new suit of armor
    armor_pieces_used_1 = 2000
    #He then uses 1/4 of the remaining armor pieces to build a second suit of armor
    armor_pieces_used_2 = (armor_pieces_total - armor_pieces_used_1) * 1/4
    #The answer is
    result = armor_pieces_total - armor_pieces_used_1 - armor_pieces_used_2
    return result

Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: In a game, LeBron James made 2-point shots 8 times and 3-point shots 3 times. 2-point shots are worth 2 points and 3-point shots are worth 3 points. How many points did LeBron James score in the game?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron made 2-point shots 8 times
    two_point_shots = 8
    #2-point shots are worth 2 points
    two_point_shot_value = 2
    #He made 3-point shots 3 times
    three_point_shots = 3
    #3-point shots are worth 3 points
    three_point_shot_value = 3
    #The answer is
    result = two_point_shots * two_point_shot_value + three_point_shots * three_point_shot_value
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 120 sticks. 1/3 of the sticks are broken. 1/4 of the sticks are new. The rest are used. How many used sticks does the team have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total sticks
    total_sticks = 120
    #Broken sticks
    broken_sticks = total_sticks / 3
    #New sticks
    new_sticks = total_sticks / 4
    #Used sticks
    used_sticks = total_sticks - broken_sticks - new_sticks
    return used_sticks

    pink_dollars_initial = 12000000000000

    pink_dollars_spent_clothes = 2000000000000
    #She then buys 500000000000 pink dollars worth of cars
    pink_dollars_spent_cars = 50000000
Topic: swimming ### Response: 
Question: A swimmer is 1000 meters from the shore. They swim 200 meters, then turn around and swim 100 meters back. They then swim 300 meters, turn around and swim 200 meters back. How far are they from the shore?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The swimmer is 1000 meters from the shore
    distance_initial = 1000
    #They swim 200 meters, then turn around and swim 100 meters back
    distance_after_1 = distance_initial - 200 + 100
    #They then swim 300 meters, turn around and swim 200 meters back
    distance_after_2 = distance_after_1 - 300 + 200
    #The answer is
    result = distance_after_2
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: 2000 people are at a train station. 1200 of them are on a train, 300 of them are on a platform, and 500 of them are in the parking lot. How many people are not at the train station?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2000 people are at a train station
    total_people = 2000
    #1200 of them are on a train
    people_on_train = 1200
    #300 of them are on a platform
    people_on_platform = 300
    #500 of them are in the parking lot
    people_in_parking_lot = 500
    #The answer is
    result = total_people - people_on_train - people_on_platform - people_in_parking_lot
    return result
Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 
There are 12 unicorns in a field. 4 of them are pink, 5 of them are purple, and the rest are blue. How many unicorns are blue?

Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 12 unicorns in a field
    unicorns_total = 12
    #4 of them are pink
    unicorns_pink = 4
    #5 of them are purple
    unicorns_purple = 5
    #The rest are blue. The answer is
    unicorns_blue = unicorns_total - unicorns_pink - unicorns_purple
    return unicorns_blue
Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The 49ers have 320 rushing yards. They have 40 more rushing yards than passing yards. How many passing yards do they have?

Solution:
def solution():

    rushing_yards = 320
    #They have 40 more rushing yards than passing yards

    return result
Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James, the greatest basketball player of all time, has 100 points. He scores 20 points in the first quarter, 15 in the second, 30 in the third, and 15 in the fourth. 
How many points does he have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron started with 100 points
    points_initial = 100
    #He scored 20 in the first quarter
    points_first_quarter = 20
    #He scored 15 in the second quarter
    points_second_quarter = 15
    #He scored 30 in the third quarter
    points_third_quarter = 30
    #He scored 15 in the fourth quarter
    points_fourth_quarter = 15
    #The answer is
    result = points_initial - points_first_quarter - points_second_quarter - points_third_quarter - points_fourth_quarter
    return result
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: There are 200 people in the gymnasium. 150 of them are wearing blue. 30 of them are wearing red. 20 of them are wearing both blue and red. How many people in the gymnasium are not wearing blue or red?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 200 people in the gymnasium
    people_total = 200
    #150 of them are wearing blue
    people_blue = 150
    #30 of them are wearing red
    people_red = 30
    #20 of them are wearing both blue and red
    people_both = 20
    #The answer is
    result = people_total - people_blue - people_red + people_both
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can punch 500 times in 10 minutes. How many times can he punch in 20 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can punch 500 times in 10 minutes
    punches_10_minutes = 500
    #20 minutes is 1200 seconds
    seconds_20_minutes = 1200
    #The answer is
    result = (punches_10_minutes / 600) * seconds_20_minutes
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 
The volleyball team has 12 players. 3 of the players are from the 11th grade. 5 of the players are from the 12th grade. The rest of the players are from the 10th grade. How many players are from the 10th grade?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of 11th graders
    eleventh_graders = 3
    #Number of 12th graders
    twelfth_graders = 5
    #The rest of the players are 10th graders
    tenth_graders = total_players - eleventh_graders - twelfth_graders
    return tenth_graders

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: 
A 747 can carry 366 passengers. A 777 can carry 300 passengers. How many more passengers can 747s carry than 777s if there are 20 747s and 15 777s?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 747 can carry 366 passengers
    passengers_747 = 366
    #A 777 can carry 300 passengers
    passengers_777 = 300
    #There are 20 747s and 15 777s
    planes_747 = 20
    planes_777 = 15
    #The answer is
    result = (passengers_747 * planes_747) - (passengers_777 * planes_777)
    return result

    #3 of the players are from the US
    players_us = 3
    #5 of the players are from Germany
    players_germany = 5
    #2 of the players are from Spain
    players_spain = 2
    #1 of the players is from the United Kingdom
    players_uk = 1
    #The answer is

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 12 players. 

Each player has 2 sticks. 

The team also has 30 sticks in a locker. 

How many sticks does the team have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A lacrosse team has 12 players
    players = 12
    #Each player has 2 sticks
    sticks_per_player = 2
    #The team also has 30 sticks in a locker
    sticks_in_locker = 30
    #The answer is
    result = players * sticks_per_player + sticks_in_locker
    return result

Question: A cheer leading squad has 20 members. 10 of them are on the pyramid, 5 of them are on the ground, and the rest are in the air. How many cheerleaders are in the air?
Solution:

    members = 20

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
def solution():
    #A herd of 100 dinosaurs is grazing. 1/4 of the dinosaurs are triceratops, 1/5 of the dinosaurs are brontosauruses, and the rest are tyrannosauruses. How many tyrannosauruses are there?
    total_dinosaurs = 100
    triceratops = total_dinosaurs / 4
    brontosauruses = total_dinosaurs / 5
    tyrannosauruses = total_dinosaurs - triceratops - brontosauruses
    return tyrannosauruses

Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 20 unicorns ate 100 apples. 15 unicorns ate 150 apples. 10 unicorns ate 50 apples. How many apples were eaten in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 unicorns ate 100 apples
    unicorns1 = 20
    apples1 = 100
    #15 unicorns ate 150 apples
    unicorns2 = 15
    apples2 = 150
    #10 unicorns ate 50 apples
    unicorns3 = 10
    apples3 = 50
    #The answer is
    result = (unicorns1 * apples1) + (unicorns2 * apples2) + (unicorns3 * apples3)
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: A car is traveling at 60 miles per hour. It is 200 miles from its destination. How many hours will it take to get there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A car is traveling at 60 miles per hour
    car_speed = 60
    #It is 200 miles from its destination
    car_distance = 200
    #The answer is
    result = car_distance / car_speed
    return result
Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: Patrick Mahomes has 1000 passing yards. 200 of them are from the 1st game, 300 of them are from the 2nd game, and the rest are from the 3rd game. How many passing yards does he have from the 3rd game?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total passing yards
    total_passing_yards = 1000
    #1st game passing yards
    first_game_passing_yards = 200
    #2nd game passing yards
    second_game_passing_yards = 300
    #3rd game passing yards is the total passing yards minus the 1st and 2nd game passing yards
    third_game_passing_yards = total_passing_yards - first_game_passing_yards - second_game_passing_yards
    return third_game_passing_yards

Topic: football ### Response: 

Question: 

- A football team has 20 players.
- 5 of the players are on the offense.
- 8 of the players are on the defense.
- 4 of the players are on special teams.
- 3 of the players are on the sidelines.

How many more players are on the field than on the sidelines?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 20
    #Offense players
    offense_players = 5
    #Defense players
    defense_players = 8
    #Special teams players
    special_teams_players = 4
    #Sidelines players
    sidelines_players = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (offense_players + defense_players + special_teams_players) - sidelines_players
    return result

Question: Cynthia has 220 Pokémon. 50% of her Pokémon are Psychic-type. 20% of the Psychic-type Pokémon are also Ghost-type. How many Psychic- and Ghost-type Pokémon does Cynthia have?

    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: 100 cars are in a parking lot. 20 of the cars are red, 30 of the cars are blue, and the rest are green. How many of the cars are green?
Solution:
def solution():
    #100 cars are in a parking lot
    cars_total = 100
    #20 of the cars are red
    cars_red = 20
    #30 of the cars are blue
    cars_blue = 30
    #The answer is
    result = cars_total - cars_red - cars_blue
    return result
Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 
Question: In the game Super Mario Bros, Mario can collect 100 coins to get an extra life. 
If he has 1000 coins, how many extra lives does he get?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Mario has 1000 coins
    coins = 1000
    #He can collect 100 coins to get an extra life. The answer is
    result = coins // 100
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
def solution():
    #A volleyball team has 12 players. 
    #3 of them are setters, 5 are hitters, and the rest are blockers.
    #How many blockers are on the team?
    total_players = 12
    setters = 3
    hitters = 5
    blockers = total_players - setters - hitters
    return blockers

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 18 Grand Slam singles titles. 5 of them are from the Australian Open, 3 are from the French Open, 7 are from Wimbledon, and the rest are from the US Open. How many of her Grand Slam singles titles are from the US Open?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 18 Grand Slam singles titles
    total_titles = 18
    #5 of them are from the Australian Open
    australian_open_titles = 5
    #3 are from the French Open
    french_open_titles = 3
    #7 are from Wimbledon
    wimbledon_titles = 7
    #The answer is
    us_open_titles = total_titles - australian_open_titles - french_open_titles - wimbledon_titles
    return us_open_titles
Topic: Pokémon ### Response: 
Question: A Pikachu weighs 13.2 pounds. A Charizard weighs 187.2 times as much as a Pikachu. How much does a Charizard weigh?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A Pikachu weighs 13.2 pounds
    pikachu_weight = 13.2
    #A Charizard weighs 187.2 times as much as a Pikachu
    charizard_weight = 187.2 * pikachu_weight
    #The answer is
    result = charizard_weight
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: 
The 49ers are a football team. 
They have 24 first downs. 
They have 3 more first downs than the Bears. 
How many first downs do the Bears have?
Solution:
def solution():

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: 300 people lined up to get ice cream. 1/3 of the people in line got a scoop of chocolate ice cream, 1/5 of the people in line got a scoop of strawberry ice cream, and the rest of the people in line got a scoop of vanilla ice cream. How many people in line got a scoop of vanilla ice cream?

Solution:
def solution():
    #300 people lined up to get ice cream
    people = 300
    #1/3 of the people in line got a scoop of chocolate ice cream
    chocolate_scoops = people / 3
    #1/5 of the people in line got a scoop of strawberry ice cream
    strawberry_scoops = people / 5
    #The answer is
    result = people - chocolate_scoops - strawberry_scoops
    return result

Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America is 6'2" tall. 12" is 1 foot. How many inches tall is Captain America?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America is 6'2" tall
    captain_america_height_feet = 6

Topic: trains ### Response: 
def solution():
    #A train is 1000 feet long
    train_length = 1000
    #200 of the feet are for the engine
    engine_length = 200
    #300 of the feet are for the coal car
    coal_car_length = 300
    #100 of the feet are for each of the 5 passenger cars
    passenger_car_length = 100
    #The rest of the train is for the caboose. The answer is
    caboose_length = train_length - engine_length - coal_car_length - (passenger_car_length * 5)
    return caboose_length
Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can bench press 2000 pounds. 

He can bench press 500 more pounds than he can squat. 

He can squat 3000 more pounds than he can deadlift. 

How much can Superman deadlift?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can bench press 2000 pounds
    bench_press = 2000
    #He can bench press 500 more pounds than he can squat
    squat = bench_press - 500
    #He can squat 3000 more pounds than he can deadlift
    deadlift = squat - 3000
    #The answer is
    result = deadlift
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response: 

Question: 

There are 1200 dogs in a city. 200 of them are in the pound. 300 of them are in shelters. 100 of them are on the streets. How many dogs are in homes?

Solution:

def solution():

    #Total dogs in the city

    total_dogs = 1200

    #Dogs in the pound

    pound_dogs = 200

    #Dogs in shelters

    shelter_dogs = 300

    #Dogs on the streets

    street_dogs = 100

    #The answer is

    result = total_dogs - pound_dogs - shelter_dogs - street_dogs

    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 

Question: Superman can fly 1000 miles per hour. He needs to fly 3000 miles to get to the Fortress of Solitude. How many hours does it take him to get there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly 1000 miles per hour
    miles_per_hour = 1000
    #He needs to fly 3000 miles to get to the Fortress of Solitude
    miles = 3000
    #The answer is

    return result
Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 

Question: 100 Fortnite players were in a match. 20 more players joined. 40% of the players were eliminated. How many players are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #100 players were in a match
    players_initial = 100
    #20 more players joined
    players_joined = 20
    #40% of the players were eliminated
    players_eliminated = 0.40
    #The answer is
    result = players_initial + players_joined - (players_initial + players_joined) * players_eliminated
    return result
Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: 
A Minecraft world is 256 blocks wide, 256 blocks long, and 128 blocks high. 
Each block is 16x16x16 voxels. 
How many voxels are in the world?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A Minecraft world is 256 blocks wide, 256 blocks long, and 128 blocks high
    blocks_wide = 256
    blocks_long = 256
    blocks_high = 128
    #Each block is 16x16x16 voxels
    voxels_per_block = 16 * 16 * 16
    #The answer is
    result = (blocks_wide * blocks_long * blocks_high) * voxels_per_block
    return result
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena has 24 Grand Slam titles. 8 of her titles are from Wimbledon. 6 are from the US Open. 5 are from the Australian Open. 5 are from the French Open. How many of her titles are from other tournaments?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena has 24 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles = 24
    #8 of her titles are from Wimbledon
    wimbledon_titles = 8
    #6 are from the US Open
    us_open_titles = 6
    #5 are from the Australian Open
    australian_open_titles = 5

    french_open_titles = 5
    #The answer is
    result = grand_slam_titles - wimbledon_titles - us_open_titles - australian_open_titles - french_open_titles
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 
A volleyball team has 12 members. 
They need to line up in 3 rows with 4 in the front and the same number in the back. 
How many people will be in the middle row?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of members
    total_members = 12
    #Number of members in the front and back row
    front_back_row = 4
    #Number of members in the middle row
    middle_row = (total_members - 2*front_back_row)
    return middle_row

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Spiderman can web-sling 1000 feet per minute. He has to web-sling 3000 feet to the top of a building. How many minutes does it take him to get to the top of the building?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can web-sling 1000 feet per minute
    spiderman_web_sling_rate = 1000
    #He has to web-sling 3000 feet to the top of a building
    spiderman_web_sling_distance = 3000
    #The answer is
    result = spiderman_web_sling_distance / spiderman_web_sling_rate
    return result
Topic: swimming ### Response: 

Question: 

A swimmer can swim 20 laps per hour. 

If she swims 3 hours a day, 5 days a week, how many laps does she swim in 4 weeks?

Solution:

def solution():
    #A swimmer can swim 20 laps per hour
    laps_per_hour = 20
    #If she swims 3 hours a day, 5 days a week
    hours_per_day = 3
    days_per_week = 5
    #How many laps does she swim in 4 weeks?
    weeks = 4
    #The answer is
    result = laps_per_hour * hours_per_day * days_per_week * weeks
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team has 45 players. 11 of the players are on the offense, 13 of the players are on the defense, and 5 of the players are on both the offense and defense. How many players are on the team but not on either the offense or defense?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 45 players
    players = 45
    #11 of the players are on the offense
    offense = 11
    #13 of the players are on the defense
    defense = 13
    #5 of the players are on both the offense and defense
    both = 5
    #The answer is
    result = players - offense - defense + both
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: A 300-car freight train is 3.5 miles long. A 60-car passenger train is 0.75 miles long. How many miles of track are needed to hold 2 of each?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 300-car freight train is 3.5 miles long
    freight_train_length = 3.5
    #A 60-car passenger train is 0.75 miles long
    passenger_train_length = 0.75
    #They need 2 of each
    num_trains = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (freight_train_length + passenger_train_length) * num_trains
    return result

Question: Steph Curry has 1000 3-point shots. He makes 500 of them. He misses 250 of them. How many of the shots are left?

    shots_initial = 1000
    #He makes 500 of them

Topic: Black Panther ### Response: 
Question: Black Panther can run at a speed of 50 mph. 

He is chasing a lion that is 200 miles away. 

If the lion is running at a speed of 30 mph, how long will it take for Black Panther to catch the lion?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther's speed
    black_panther_speed = 50
    #Lion's speed
    lion_speed = 30
    #Distance
    distance = 200
    #The answer is
    result = distance / (black_panther_speed - lion_speed)
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response: 

Question: A soccer team has 20 players. 40% of the players are from the 10th grade, 30% are from the 11th grade, and the rest are from the 12th grade. How many 12th graders are on the team?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of players
    total_players = 20
    #40% of the players are from the 10th grade
    tenth_grade_players = 0.40 * total_players
    #30% of the players are from the 11th grade
    eleventh_grade_players = 0.30 * total_players
    #The rest are from the 12th grade
    twelfth_grade_players = total_players - tenth_grade_players - eleventh_grade_players
    #The answer is
    result = twelfth_grade_players
    return result

3 of them are setters, 

4 of them are hitters, 

2 of them are blockers, 

and the rest are liberos. 

How many liberos are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #The number of setters, hitters, and blockers
    setters = 3
    hitters = 4
    blockers = 2
    #The number of liberos is
    liberos = total_players - setters - hitters - blockers
    return liberos
Topic: swimming ### Response: 

def solution():
    # A swimmer can swim 1000 meters in 10 minutes.
    # How many meters can the swimmer swim in 20 minutes?

    # 1000 meters in 10 minutes is a rate of 100 meters per minute
    rate = 1000 / 10
    # 20 minutes is 20 * 60 = 1200 seconds
    time = 20 * 60
    # The answer is
    result = rate * time
    return result
Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 10 unicorns ate 100 apples. 15 unicorns ate 150 apples. 20 unicorns ate 200 apples. How many unicorns ate 250 apples?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 unicorns ate 100 apples
    unicorns_100_apples = 10
    #15 unicorns ate 150 apples
    unicorns_150_apples = 15
    #20 unicorns ate 200 apples
    unicorns_200_apples = 20
    #The answer is
    result = (unicorns_100_apples * 150) / 100
    return result

    fans_total = 1000000000
    #100000000 of them are in the US
    fans_us = 100000000
    #50000000 are in the UK

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: A cheerleading squad has 20 members. 5 of the members are on the A-squad, 8 are on the B-squad, and the rest are on the C-squad. How many members are on the C-squad?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The cheerleading squad has 20 members
    total_members = 20
    #5 of the members are on the A-squad
    a_squad = 5
    #8 are on the B-squad
    b_squad = 8
    #The rest are on the C-squad
    c_squad = total_members - a_squad - b_squad
    return c_squad
Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 
Question: 
There are 6 Power Rangers. 2 of them are Red, 2 of them are Blue, and 2 of them are Yellow. How many Power Rangers are not Red?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total Power Rangers
    total_power_rangers = 6
    #2 of them are Red
    red_power_rangers = 2
    #2 of them are Blue
    blue_power_rangers = 2
    #2 of them are Yellow
    yellow_power_rangers = 2
    #The answer is
    result = total_power_rangers - red_power_rangers
    return result
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 23 Grand Slam singles titles. 

She has 14 Grand Slam doubles titles with her sister, Venus. 

She has 2 Grand Slam mixed doubles titles. 

How many Grand Slam titles does she have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena has 23 Grand Slam singles titles
    singles_titles = 23
    #14 Grand Slam doubles titles with her sister, Venus
    doubles_titles = 14
    #2 Grand Slam mixed doubles titles
    mixed_doubles_titles = 2
    #The answer is
    result = singles_titles + doubles_titles + mixed_doubles_titles
    return result
Topic: ice cream ### Response: 

Question: 

A 3-scoop ice cream cone has 150 calories. 

A 4-scoop ice cream cone has 200 calories. 

How many calories are in a 5-scoop ice cream cone?

Solution:

def solution():

# 3-scoop ice cream cone has 150 calories

scoop1 = 150

# 4-scoop ice cream cone has 200 calories

scoop2 = 200

# 5-scoop ice cream cone has 

scoop3 = (scoop2 - scoop1) / 1

result = scoop3 * 5

return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: 
In the first year, there were 1000 students at Hogwarts. The next year, 200 more students enrolled. The year after that, 300 students left. The year after that, 400 more students enrolled. How many students are now at Hogwarts?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Initial number of students
    students_initial = 1000
    #200 more students enrolled in the next year
    students_enrolled_next_year = 200
    #300 students left in the year after that
    students_left_next_year = 300
    #400 more students enrolled in the year after that
    students_enrolled_next_next_year = 400
    #The answer is
    result = students_initial + students_enrolled_next_year - students_left_next_year + students_enrolled_next_next_year
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response: 

Question:

A bakery bakes 1200 cookies. 

They bake 200 more cookies on Monday, 300 more on Tuesday, and 400 more on Wednesday. 

How many cookies do they have now?
Solution:

def solution():
    #The bakery bakes 1200 cookies
    cookies_initial = 1200
    #They bake 200 more cookies on Monday
    cookies_baked_monday = 200
    #They bake 300 more on Tuesday
    cookies_baked_tuesday = 300
    #They bake 400 more on Wednesday
    cookies_baked_wednesday = 400
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_initial + cookies_baked_monday + cookies_baked_tuesday + cookies_baked_wednesday
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question: 1000 Fortnite players are in a match. 200 of them are from the United States, 150 of them are from Canada, and 120 of them are from Mexico. How many of them are from other countries?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1000 Fortnite players are in a match
    total_players = 1000
    #200 of them are from the United States
    players_us = 200
    #150 of them are from Canada
    players_canada = 150

Question: The Cannons have 1200 fans. 200 of them are from the city. 400 of them are from the suburbs. 600 of them are from the country. How many of the Cannons' fans are not from the city or the suburbs?

    fans_total = 1200
    #200 of them are from the city
    fans_city = 200
    #400 of them are from the suburbs
    fans_suburbs = 400

Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James has 1000 points. He scores 200 points in the first game, 300 in the second game, and 400 in the third game. How many points does he have left?

    points_initial = 1000
    #He scores 200 points in the first game
    points_first_game = 200
    #300 in the second game
    points_second_game = 300
    #and 400 in the third game
    points_third_game = 400
    #The answer is

    return result

    #30% from the right side

    #20% from the center

    #The answer is
    result
Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: 200 cats are at the cat cafe. 30 cats are asleep. 60 cats are eating. 20 cats are playing. 10 cats are grooming. How many cats are doing other things?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cats
    total_cats = 200
    #Cats asleep
    cats_asleep = 30
    #Cats eating
    cats_eating = 60
    #Cats playing
    cats_playing = 20
    #Cats grooming
    cats_grooming = 10
    #Cats doing other things
    cats_other = total_cats - cats_asleep - cats_eating - cats_playing - cats_grooming
    return cats_other

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: 
LeBron James has 5000 points. He has 1200 more than 4 times the number of rebounds he has. How many rebounds does he have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James has 5000 points
    points = 5000
    #He has 1200 more than 4 times the number of rebounds he has
    rebounds = (points - 1200) / 4
    return rebounds

He spends 20 coins on a mushroom. 

He spends 30 coins on a flower.

    #He spends 20 coins on a mushroom
    coins_mushroom = 20

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman has 2000 spider-webs. He uses 1000 spider-webs to trap a villain. He then uses 200 spider-webs to swing from building to building. How many spider-webs does he have left?
Solution:

    #Spiderman started with 2000 spider-webs
    spider_webs_initial = 2000
    #He used 1000 spider-webs to trap a villain
    spider_webs_used_trap = 1000
    #He used 200 spider-webs to swing from building to building
    spider_webs_used_swing = 200

    return result
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: The field hockey team has 12 players. 3 of the players are 16 years old, 5 are 17, 2 are 18, and the rest are 15. How many players are 15?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #16-year-old players
    sixteen_year_old = 3
    #17-year-old players
    seventeen_year_old = 5
    #18-year-old players
    eighteen_year_old = 2
    #15-year-old players
    fifteen_year_old = total_players - sixteen_year_old - seventeen_year_old - eighteen_year_old
    return fifteen_year_old
Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America is 6.25 feet tall. 1.5 of his feet are in his legs. 1.5 of his feet are in his arms. The rest of his height is in his torso. How many feet of Captain America are in his torso?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America is 6.25 feet tall
    captain_america_height = 6.25
    #1.5 of his feet are in his legs
    legs_height = 1.5
    #1.5 of his feet are in his arms
    arms_height = 1.5
    #The rest of his height is in his torso
    torso_height = captain_america_height - legs_height - arms_height
    return torso_height
